Every time I have had to call, I have sat on hold for a minimum of 1 to 4 hours, only to have my call "dropped" just I finally reached a live person!.
My advice to anyone who has to call this call center; prior to disclosing why you are calling, make sure you have the person who answers take down your name and call back number. Then get their commitment that they will call you back in the likely event there is a disconnect. Otherwise, if your reason for calling is too complicated or requires. more of an effort from them than just basic data entry (like updating an address), there is a good chance your call will be "conveniently" dropped. Of course, the worker, unable to identify who they were just talking to,  will have no choice but to forget about you and move to the next client waiting  on hold. You will be left frustrated, inconvenienced and unaccomplished in whatever it was prompting your call in the first place. You will have gotten nowhere and taken all day to get there. The real inconvenience will be in having to wait until the following day, the next week, or worse, until after their "paid" holiday to get your medical insurance approved, your money released or your food stamps loaded on your card. Too bad for you if your surgery gets postponed because you have no insurance coverage, your baby goes without diapers for a day, or your next meal won't happen for another 4 days. At least all the over compensated folks essentially paid to hang up on you will get their much  "needed" rest before they return to the grulling task of picking and choosing who they are going to help!<//Text>

< Review>
Unfortunately, bad management has dragged this great track down over the last couple years. Played early and battled sprinklers in the middle of the fairways on multiple holes and maintenance drowning the greens and bunkers while waiting to hit our approach shots. Took relief from puddles in the fairways from the sprinklers being on so long. They definitely could've done the watering well before the first tee times, or stayed a couple holes ahead of the first group. Fairways are pretty beat up and weeds are taking over the entire course. Greens rolled nice, but were very soft. Tee boxes were not mown tight enough for iron shots on par 3 holes. Bunkers are basically dirt or mud. If you play in the late afternoon, be prepared to get kicked off the course with plenty of light left. They care more about saving payroll than serving customers. The price makes it bearable, but some of these issues are avoidable with proper management.<//Review>

< review>
The original location of Westlake Coffee Shop used to be near the Westlake Library until the business temporarily shut down for a few years back in the early 2000s. Then, Westlake Coffee Shop relocated near Century Theater where there's more foot traffic.

When Westlake Coffee Shop used to be located in Westlake itself, I was a student at OLM. I would stop by almost everyday after school for a bite to eat or do my homework. The waitresses didn't mind and were very hospitable. Flash forward and now Westlake Coffee Shop moved to a different part of Daly City where there are better parking options. Waitresses have changed obviously, but that 50s vibe remained.

I enjoy coming here on Sunday mornings for breakfast. I often order their Westlake Special with hash browns. I've tried their burgers, which are pretty dry. I've also tried their omelettes, which are very filling. Decently priced meals. Friendly management. You can even order take out if you don't want to dine in. Overall, nice place to have breakfast or lunch until they close at 3pm.< /review>
